###  Tsekki₁

This rare proper noun overlaps more common *Tsekki* (FIXME)
* UPOS:  PROPN
* in KOTUS dictionary under:  5
* Origin:  joukahainen
* Possible NER class:  GEO
* Blacklisted:  PROPN-BLOCKING
